| ✅ | GH#29 | **Status change bug — doesn't stick when duplicate/related RO exists** | **Production bug reported by managers/techs + witnessed by Roland Session 51.** **Root cause (fixed v1.408):** 13 write-path lookups resolved `currentFilteredData[index]` back to `currentData` via `findIndex(item => item.customerName === ro.customerName && item.dateReceived === ro.dateReceived)`. With duplicate (name, date) pairs, `findIndex` returned the FIRST match — every write silently targeted the wrong row. Affected functions: `updateROStatus`, `updateROUrgency`, `updateROProgress`, `editField`, `uploadPhoto`, `uploadDocument`, `setMainPhoto`, `archiveRO`, `openScheduleModal`, `confirmSchedule`, `proceedWithSchedule`, `openPartsModal`, `openEditRO`. **Fix (v1.408):** UUID-first lookup `ro._supabaseId ? findIndex(item._supabaseId === ro._supabaseId) : fallback(name+date)`. `_supabaseId` populated from Supabase `row.id` at load time on every RO (lines 10221, 10339); fallback only fires for legacy data. Applied via `patch_status_bug.py`. **Part 2 (DB cleanup) split out as GH#29b below.** | ✅ Code shipped v1.408 (Session 51) |

| ✅ | — | **Cashiered archiver — ROOT-CAUSED + FIXED Session 73 (3 latent bugs from Session 61)** | **Way bigger than the Session 71 surface read.** The "2 stuck rows" was the visible tip of a 4-week-old systemic failure. Session 73 schema-discovery revealed 32 rows stuck in Delivered/Cashed Out, not 2. **3 latent bugs in the original `cron_archive_cashiered_ros.sql` (Session 61):** Bug #1: function referenced `ro_row.customer_phone/_email/_address` but actual columns on `repair_orders` are `phone/email/address` — `record "ro_row" has no field "customer_phone"`. All 3 latent since 2026-04-29; bug #1 killed the function before #2/#3 fired, so the cron silently rolled back every Saturday for ~4 weeks. **Fix:** added `UNIQUE (original_ro_id)` constraint to `cashiered` (pre-check + idempotent), corrected column names, wrapped insurance_data cast in `BEGIN/EXCEPTION` block. | ✅ | GH#42 | **Fix Step 2 fallback bypass of loadUserRoles (completes Lynn admin-button fix)** | **Shipped v1.417 (Session 70, 2026-05-21, commit `c9b21a8`).** Second silent-demote bug discovered after v1.416 deployed but Lynn still saw only 2 buttons (Closed ROs + Time Off) the next morning. v1.416 hardened `loadUserRoles()` internals but a separate code path bypassed `loadUserRoles()` entirely. Session-restore Step 2 ("Fall back to Google token if Supabase session gone") set `sessionRestoredFromCache=true`, then the One Tap prompt skip-condition keyed on that flag — preventing the signInWithIdToken callback from ever firing, so `supabaseSession` stayed null, `userRoles` stayed `[]`, every `isAdmin()`/`hasRole()` gate failed. The flag was meant to mean "we're logged in" but actually only meant "we restored *something* from cache" — true even when only a stale Google token had been restored. Fit Lynn's intermittent multi-day pattern: Supabase JWTs expire ~hourly, Google token lasts 1+ hr; overnight tab can have dead Supabase + warm Google. **5 surgical edits to index.html:** (1) `getUserInfo()` awaits `loadUserRoles()` before first paint, (2) Step 2 fallback awaits `loadUserRoles()` before `updateViewModeDropdown()`, (3) callback skip narrowed from `sessionRestoredFromCache \|\| supabaseSession` → just `supabaseSession`, (4) post-`signInWithIdToken` success now re-runs `loadUserRoles` + `updateViewModeDropdown` + `updateAuthStatus(true)`, (5) One Tap prompt skip flipped from `!sessionRestoredFromCache` → `!supabaseSession`. `sessionRestoredFromCache` preserved for non-auth UI hydration but no longer used as proxy for "RBAC is active". worklist-report.html and customer-checkin.html unchanged (no Step 2 path). Trace of fixed flow: Step 2 fires → loadUserRoles returns [] (anon RLS) → buttons momentarily hidden → One Tap prompt fires (NEW) → auto_select picks account → callback fires → signInWithIdToken succeeds → supabaseSession populated → loadUserRoles re-runs with valid session → userRoles populated → updateViewModeDropdown re-renders → admin buttons appear. | ✅ Done — Session 70 |

## ⚠️ Archived — Resolved Known Issues

### ~~Dead Kenect code still live in index.html~~ — RESOLVED v1.445 (Session 92, 2026-06-05)

All dead Kenect UI/JS removed in the Session 92 teardown (greppable `[KENECT TEARDOWN v1.445 S92]` markers). **Two lessons preserved:** (1) The April 2026 "Kenect Removal" deleted the repo file but NOT the dashboard UI/JS — AND, discovered Session 92, NOT the deployed Supabase function either: `kenect-proxy` sat ACTIVE on Supabase for 2 months after its source was deleted. **When tearing down an edge function, always verify with `supabase functions list` — deleting the repo file does nothing to the deployment.** (2) Regex-based bulk deletion of JS functions is brace-fragile: a non-greedy `.*?\}` match truncated 3 of the Session 92 deletions at the first standalone `}` line, leaving orphan fragments. The `node --check` syntax gate caught all 3 — never skip it after scripted edits.

The flag was meant to mean "we're logged in" but actually only meant "we restored *something* from cache" — true even when only a stale Google token had been restored. Pattern fit Lynn's "intermittent over multiple days" symptom: Supabase JWTs expire ~hourly; tabs left open overnight can have a dead Supabase session but a still-warm Google token (1+ hr grace), triggering Step 2. **Fix (v1.417, commit `c9b21a8`):** 5 surgical edits to index.html — (1) `getUserInfo()` awaits `loadUserRoles()` before first paint, (2) Step 2 fallback awaits `loadUserRoles()` before `updateViewModeDropdown()`, (3) callback skip narrowed from `sessionRestoredFromCache || supabaseSession` → just `supabaseSession`, (4) post-`signInWithIdToken` success now re-runs `loadUserRoles` + `updateViewModeDropdown` + `updateAuthStatus(true)`, (5) One Tap prompt skip flipped from `!sessionRestoredFromCache` → `!supabaseSession`. ## ⚠️ Archived — Historical Known Issues (removed / superseded systems)

> Relocated 2026-06-14 (Session 107): Twilio A2P teardown, Kenect/Slack removal, and the 2026-04-11 S2–S7 security-remediation build notes. Kept here for historical reference only.

### Slack Integration (v1.403, GH#20)
- `notifySlack(eventType, payload)` in index.html is **fire-and-forget** — non-2xx responses from the Edge Function are silently swallowed (only network errors caught). If a trigger seems to not fire, check Network tab for response status.
- Status change notifications only wired for "Ready for pickup" — all other status transitions intentionally have no Slack trigger (by design, deferred).
- Edge Function `slack-notify` v1.2 uses **origin-only auth** — validates `origin === 'https://patriotsrv.github.io'`. `SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` is NOT used for auth on the Edge Function side.
- Chrome DevTools console paste warning is unrelated to Slack — cosmetic only.
- **Slack Workspace:** Patriots RV Services. **App:** PRVS Dashboard (App ID: A0AS6TYHZKM).
- **Channels:** `#parts-alerts`, `#ro-updates`, `#warranty-flags` — webhook URLs stored as Supabase Secrets (not committed to repo)
- **Supabase Secrets:** `SLACK_WEBHOOK_PARTS_ALERTS`, `SLACK_WEBHOOK_RO_UPDATES`, `SLACK_WEBHOOK_WARRANTY_FLAGS`

### `isAdmin()` — Now Role-Based (S2 complete 2026-04-11)
- **All 5 HTML files migrated:** `isAdmin()` now checks `userRoles.includes('Admin')` via Supabase `user_roles` table — no hardcoded email arrays anywhere.
- **`loadUserRoles()`** must be awaited before any `isAdmin()` / `isManagerOrAdmin()` / `hasRole()` call. All auth flows (DOMContentLoaded, handleSignIn/handleGoogleSignIn) already do this.
- **`_allStaff`** (from `staff` table) used for operational role lookups (sr_manager badge, silo grouping, admin exclusion from reports). Separate from `userRoles` (which is RBAC permissions).
- **Old fallback pattern `isAdmin() || ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(...)` is dead** — do not reintroduce.

### claude-vision-proxy Edge Function (S4)
- **Must be deployed via CLI** before the estimate scanner works: `supabase functions deploy claude-vision-proxy`
- Uses same `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` secret as `roof-lookup` — already set in Supabase.
- Client sends `apikey: SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` header so Supabase gateway validates JWT before the function runs. Function also verifies JWT server-side via `auth.getUser()`.
- The 120-line system prompt stays client-side in `callClaudeVision()` — update it in index.html, no redeploy needed.
- `scan-api-key-bar` CSS class is dead but intentionally left in the stylesheet.

### DEBUG-Gated Logging (S5)
- `const DEBUG = false;` + `log()`/`warn()` wrappers defined near top of each HTML file. All `console.log`/`console.warn` routed through these (except `console.error` which stays direct).
- The helper bodies MUST use `console.log`/`console.warn` directly — never `log()`/`warn()` (infinite recursion bug hit during S5, fixed).
- 3 sensitive log lines permanently deleted (token preview, extracted data, id_token).

### Event Delegation on Card Template (S6)
- `#boardGrid` has delegated click + change listeners. Card template uses `data-action` + `data-idx`/`data-sid`/`data-field` attributes instead of inline onclick/onchange.
- 170+ onclick attributes remain outside the card template (modal buttons, header buttons, etc.) — Phase 2 scope if needed.
- The delegated change listener handles `parts-status-change` action from the `<select>` in the parts chip.

### CORS Origin Validation (S7)
- All 5 Edge Functions use `ALLOWED_ORIGIN = 'https://patriotsrv.github.io'` + `getCorsHeaders(req)` that checks `req.headers.get('origin')`.
- Non-matching origins get `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: ''` (empty string) — browser blocks the response.
- **Edge Functions must be redeployed** for CORS changes to take effect. Code is committed but runtime still has old `*` CORS.

### Toast System (2026-04-11)
- `showToast(message, type, options)` — types: `success` (green), `warning` (amber), `danger` (red), `info` (blue). Default auto-dismiss 4s. Options: `duration`, `action` (label+handler for confirm-style toasts), `persistent: true`.
- Toast CSS + JS wrapped in IIFE at top of index.html. Toast container `#toast-container` is fixed top-right, stacks vertically.
- 3 `confirm()` calls intentionally preserved: archive RO (line ~4327), delete field (~4529), delete part (~6445). These are destructive actions that need blocking confirmation.
- `showToast()` count after dead code cleanup: 116 (8 calls were inside dead functions that got removed).
- `toast-slide-in` keyframe (280ms cubic-bezier) shared with scanMilestoneBanner animation.

### Compact Manager View (2026-04-11)
- View mode system: `viewPresets` object defines field visibility per mode. `currentViewMode` stored in localStorage. `setViewMode()` → `applyViewPreset()` → `renderBoard()`.
- Compact template is a separate branch in `renderBoard()`'s `filtered.map()` callback — returns early when `currentViewMode === 'compact'`. Standard card template is completely untouched.
- Compact cards use `.ro-card-compact` class (not `.ro-card`). Any code using `querySelectorAll('.ro-card')` won't find compact cards. `scrollToROInBoard()` was fixed to also match `.ro-card-compact[data-ro-index]`.
- Photo upload progress (line ~4008) uses `.ro-card` to find cards — in compact mode cards won't be found, but photo upload buttons don't exist in compact view so this is a non-issue (null guard handles it).
- Event delegation works because it uses `e.target.closest('[data-action]')` and `el.closest('[data-ro-index]')` — class-agnostic selectors.
- Compact grid toggles via `grid.classList.toggle('compact-grid', currentViewMode === 'compact')`.

### Unified Search (2026-04-12)
- Search bar at top of board filters across 10 fields: customerName, roId, rv, vin, technicianAssigned, repairDescription, parkingSpot, customerPhone, customerEmail, repairType.
- Haystack approach: fields `.filter(Boolean).join(' ').toLowerCase()` then `.includes(needle)`. Space delimiter prevents cross-field bridging.
- `currentSearchFilter` variable and `setupEventListeners()` wiring unchanged — search input `id="customerSearch"` preserved for backward compatibility.
- Post-render highlight: `highlightSearchMatches(grid, needle)` uses TreeWalker on text nodes, wraps first match per node in `<mark class="search-highlight">`. Skips SCRIPT/STYLE/INPUT/SELECT/TEXTAREA/MARK elements. Runs after `grid.innerHTML = ...` only when `currentSearchFilter` is active.
- Highlight is safe with escapeHtml — operates on rendered DOM after HTML entities are already resolved. Does NOT inject into template literals.
- Multi-word search (e.g. "john roof") only matches if those exact consecutive characters appear in the joined haystack — this is expected V1 behavior, not a bug.
- Compact view: haystack filter works on all 10 ro.* fields regardless of view mode. Highlight only applies to fields visible in the rendered template (customer, RO ID, RV, tech, spot in compact; more fields in standard).

### Dead Code Cleanup (2026-04-11)
- **968 lines removed** across 4 commits. index.html went from 13,997 → 13,128 lines (-869). solar.html went from 6,393 → 6,354 lines (-39).
- Spec: `docs/specs/DEAD_CODE_CLEANUP_SPEC.md` — 3 phases with verification scripts.
- Dynamic CSS classes preserved (never remove): `status-*`, `urgency-*`, `toast-*`, `ro-card-status-*`.
- `_doMarkPartsOrdered` was orphaned by the removal of `markPartsOrdered` in a prior session — caught and removed in Phase 2.

### Calendar Config Table (S7)
- `app_config` table stores calendar IDs (key/value). `getCalendarId(serviceType)` checks `_appConfig` cache first, falls back to `CALENDAR_IDS_FALLBACK` constant.
- `loadAppConfig()` called in both auth paths (SSO success + session restore). Must complete before calendar features work.
- **Migration `app_config_table.sql` must be run in Supabase SQL Editor** before the config table exists.

### solar.html Auth — Partial (S3, GH#17 pending)
- solar.html has NO login gate and NO Google sign-in flow. It creates a Supabase client with `storageKey: 'prvs_solar_auth'` and attempts to restore an existing session via `getSession()`, but there is no way to CREATE a session on this page.
- The ER genie lamp submit is guarded with `!supabaseSession` and shows a clear error message directing the user to sign in on the main dashboard first.
- GH#17 tracks adding full Google sign-in to solar.html. Until then, solar's core features (quoting, PDF, projects) work without auth via permissive anon RLS on `solar_project_store` and `solar_settings`.

### Kenect — REMOVED (2026-04-11)

- MODULARIZATION_ROADMAP.md Phase 16 (kenect.js) marked as REMOVED.

### Perplexity Computer Skills (Session 48)
- **`prvs-dashboard-startup`** — custom Perplexity skill. Triggers on "Start Session", "COMET STARTUP", "PRVS startup", etc. Clones/pulls repo, reads CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md, confirms version, reads TODO list by priority, reports last completed, waits for updates.
- **`prvs-dashboard-endsession`** — custom Perplexity skill. Triggers on "End Session", "Wrap up", "Shut it down", etc. Runs backup.sh, updates both context files, commits, pushes, confirms hash.
- Both skills persist across all Perplexity sessions (account-level). Manageable at perplexity.ai/computer/skills.

### Twilio A2P Rejection — Error 30909 / MESSAGE_FLOW (Session 55, 2026-04-25, TWO rejections)
- **What gets rejected (1st rejection cause):** Any A2P 10DLC Campaign Message Flow that describes consent as "verbal" — TCR reviewers cannot verify verbal consent. There is no artifact to screenshot. They will reject every time.
- **What gets rejected (2nd rejection cause — even bigger learning):** A signed paper consent form is offline / not publicly verifiable. Even if you attach the PDF to the Twilio Campaign as supporting documentation, TCR rejects it because the evidence "cannot be verified" without a publicly accessible URL they can navigate to in an incognito browser. The consent flow itself must be hosted publicly — not just downloadable, but visible on the page. Twilio's exact wording: "missing publicly accessible screenshots of the consent flow."
- **What actually works for TCR:** A public webpage on the company website (e.g. `patriotsrvservices.com/sms-consent`) that contains: (a) the full consent form text on-page (not behind a download), (b) all 5 mandatory disclosures (sender, types, frequency, rates, STOP/HELP) visible inline, (c) links to privacy policy + terms of service, (d) a downloadable PDF of the form, (e) a publicly hosted screenshot of a signed example. The Message Flow text in Twilio Console then references this URL so a reviewer can click straight to the evidence. This is the 3rd-attempt strategy for PRVS.
- **Other valid TCR-verifiable opt-in flows:** Web form with explicit opt-in checkbox + disclosure copy (screenshot of the live form), or two-way keyword opt-in (e.g. customer texts JOIN, receives confirmation). All require public verifiability — the test is "can a TCR reviewer navigate to it in incognito mode without login or permission?"
- **Mixed-scope trap:** "Low Volume Mixed" use case pulls TCR into reviewing BOTH employee AND customer opt-in paths — even if you only intend to send to one group right now. Solution: re-scope Campaign to a single audience (employee-only is the fastest path for PRVS) and remove all customer-related language from Campaign Description, Sample Messages, AND Message Flow. Conflicting scope across fields is itself a rejection trigger.
- **Sample messages must match scope:** Don't leave a customer-facing sample (ready-for-pickup, etc.) in the form if your Campaign Description says employee-only. TCR reads the whole submission as a unit.
- **Re-vetting timeline:** 1-5 business days from each resubmit. Approval/rejection email comes from TCR via Twilio.
- **3rd-strike risk is real:** Repeated rejections make TCR review more cautious. Don't submit speculatively — make sure the public consent page is actually live and accessible from incognito BEFORE clicking Update on the Campaign for the 3rd time.
- **Reusable workflow for future A2P submissions:** (1) Pick single audience scope (employee-only OR customer-only — never mixed at first). (2) Build a public webpage hosting the consent flow. (3) Make sure all 5 mandatory disclosures live on the page text itself, not just in linked PDFs. (4) Add cross-links from privacy + terms pages to the consent page (helps verifiability). (5) Test in incognito before submitting. (6) Reference the public URL in the Message Flow field. (7) Make sure Sample Messages, Campaign Description, and Message Flow all describe the SAME audience consistently.

### Twilio A2P 10DLC Registration (Session 53, 2026-04-21)
- **PENDING VETTING** — Campaign submitted 2026-04-21. TCR review typically 1-5 business days. No SMS can send until Campaign flips to "Approved." Roland gets email notification.

If we ever need sticky-sender or geographic routing for scale, switch to `MessagingServiceSid = MGf1da...` in `twilio-sms/index.ts`.

Managed by Roland's other Claude Project; don't modify from this project.

### Twilio SMS Stage 1 Skeleton (Session 53) — DORMANT until Roland sets secrets
- Edge functions `twilio-sms` + `twilio-webhook` committed but not deployed. They return 503 until `TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID` / `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN` / `TWILIO_PHONE_NUMBER` are set.
- **New-number path, not port:** Roland buys a fresh 10DLC number to fast-track tech SMS (~1 week). Port of main line remains GH#1 (blocked, 2-4 weeks); that's for customer SMS in Stage 3.
- A2P 10DLC registration is required before carriers will accept outbound SMS at scale (since Sep 2023). $4 brand + $15 vetting + ~$2/mo campaign. Approval 1-5 days.
- `twilio-webhook` validates Twilio signature via HMAC-SHA1 per Twilio security docs. Don't skip this — the webhook returns TwiML replies that charge Roland's account on every hit.
- Deploy webhook with `--no-verify-jwt` (Twilio posts carry no JWT). `twilio-sms` deploys normally (JWT verified).
- Webhook URL: `https://axfejhudchdejoiwaetq.supabase.co/functions/v1/twilio-webhook` — configure in Twilio console → Phone Numbers → Active → [Number] → Messaging → A MESSAGE COMES IN.
- Reply routes: `YES`/`Y` → stamps `extended_at = NOW()` on tech's currently-open session (extends 1h). `OUT`/`CLOCKOUT`/`CLOCK OUT`/`DONE` → closes session with `close_reason='tech_sms_reply'`. `STOP`/`STOPALL`/`UNSUBSCRIBE`/`CANCEL`/`END`/`QUIT` → clears `staff.sms_opt_in_at` (A2P compliance). Anything else → gentle help reply.
- **Stage 2 (after Roland's Twilio setup):** schedule pg_cron `remind-open-time-logs` M-F 21:45 UTC (4:45 PM CDT) that queries open `time_logs`, looks up phone via `staff.phone_number`, invokes `twilio-sms` with the shift-end message body, stamps `reminded_at = NOW()`.

Branch refactor/qr-phase-13, FF pre-prod (`855bf80`) -> FF main, tag v1.438. Prod main `855bf80`, rollback `7c7e6af`. PROD regression PASSED (v1.438 badge + boot line app.js:73, PRVS_QR 3 fns, `window.openQRModal===PRVS_QR.openQRModal` etc. true, 83 RVs / 83 DOM cards, Admin RBAC, zero app-origin errors). **Phase 14 `js/work-list.js` (v1.439, 13 Manager Work List fns: daysSinceAddedToWorkList, toggleWorkListPanel, _populateManagerPicker, loadWorkList, addToWorkList, _showSiloPickerForAdd, _addToWorkListWithSilo, removeFromWorkList, _saveWorkListOrder, _initWorkListBtn, _renderWorkListSiloTabs, _setWorkListSilo, renderWorkList)** extracted VERBATIM (byte-identical 13/13; node --check clean) + window bridge; inline copies retained; app.js imports it (window.PRVS_WorkList). The roadmap's 5-fn list was stale/incomplete; isSrOrAdmin (legacy alias) is interspersed in the same source block and was EXCLUDED. **CAUGHT + FIXED A REAL REGRESSION at the local-test gate:** Roland's first test showed the work list rendering empty AND other managers' lists invisible. Root cause: `_workListActiveSilo` (referenced 11x by the work-list fns) was NEVER declared with let/const/var — an undeclared implicit global. Harmless in the non-strict inline `<script>` (implicit-global assignment), but ES modules are ALWAYS strict mode, so `_workListActiveSilo = null` at the top of the module's `loadWorkList` threw `ReferenceError` BEFORE the try/catch, aborting the load (so _workListData never populated, renderWorkList never ran). An audit confirmed it was the ONLY implicit global (the other 3 state vars were declared; class/onclick/style were HTML-attr false positives). Fix: declared `let _workListActiveSilo = null;` inline next to its siblings (shared with the module via the global lexical env, same mechanism as Phase 7 currentData / Phase 11 timeLogsData). After the fix Roland confirmed the list populates, the manager picker loads other managers' lists, and dedup works (the duplicate rows he saw were test-data created during the broken window when _workListData was empty so `_showSiloPickerForAdd`'s already-added guard had nothing to compare against; cleared after the fix). Branch refactor/work-list-phase-14, FF pre-prod (`7787448`) -> FF main, tag v1.439. Prod main `7787448`, rollback `855bf80`. PROD regression PASSED (v1.439 badge + boot app.js, PRVS_WorkList 13 fns, identity true for toggle/load/render, `_workListActiveSilo` declared, qr.js intact, 83 RVs / 83 DOM cards on warm reload, Admin+SrMgr, zero app-origin errors — the wall of LastPass/Stripe/Gmail `Cannot create item with duplicate id` console lines are all browser-extension noise, not the app). **LESSON (added to Known Issues):** byte-identical extraction is necessary but NOT sufficient — pre-scan Phases 15/17/18 target fns for bare assignments to undeclared identifiers and declare them inline BEFORE extracting. **Grooming:** closed the Not-on-Lot pipeline GH#26/27/28 (fixed via the refactoring, Roland's call); closed the entire GitHub Releases backlog (18 rows; Roland is caught up) + the prvs-end-session skill-patch item + Supabase log-retention (already satisfied by the Pro plan's automatic 7-day retention — no toggle exists; Log Drains is a paid export feature, not needed); logged a `manager_work_lists(manager_email, ro_id, service_silo)` UNIQUE-constraint hardening TODO (client-side dedup only today; same class as GH#33). **Sync Gate Case B** (v1.438 + v1.439 both shipped to main this session; tags pushed during the session; the End-Session doc commit rides the same FF). Proposed and got buy-in on a 3-tier branch model: `main` = production (auto-deploys to GitHub Pages), `pre-prod` = default working/integration (Roland tests locally here before promoting), `refactor/<topic>` / `feature/<topic>` = isolated high-risk work targeting pre-prod (auth, RLS, schema migrations, big multi-file refactors), `hotfix/<topic>` = emergency-only production patch with **mandatory same-session back-merge to pre-prod** (Rule #1 of drift prevention, non-negotiable). 8 drift prevention rules codified: (1) mandatory back-merge after hotfix; (2) drift check at session start (`git log main..pre-prod` AND `git log pre-prod..main` both empty); (3) hotfix log table maintained; (4) hotfix commit message convention `HOTFIX:` prefix + tag `hotfix-YYYY-MM-DD-<slug>`; (5) tag every release with `v1.XXX`; (6) delete merged branches local + remote post-merge; (7) cap topic branch life at 7 days (weekly back-merge pre-prod INTO branch if longer); (8) forward-only flow (feature → pre-prod → main forward; hotfix → main → pre-prod back-merge). **Repo cleanup:** created `pre-prod` from main HEAD, deleted 7 stale branches local + remote (refactor/auth-phase-4.5, refactor/ro-card-phase1, wo-redesign, backup/pre-security-s1, refactor/modularization-phase-0, perplexity/safe-fixes-2026-04-10, perplexity/specs-2026-04-10). - ✅ **checkin.html v1.33 — Ghost-write to repair_orders.status FIXED + casing bug FIXED (2026-05-22, Session 71, commit `f168970`)**: Resolves both GH#29c (Session 67 reopened) and GH#29d (Session 67 investigation TODO) in a single surgical commit. Two independent bugs in the tech clockIn path, both originating in commit `b5ed919` (2026-03-08 "Add files via upload") and confirmed via `git blame` + `git log --pickaxe-regex` to NOT be Claude regressions — important for restoring Roland's confidence after he opened the session worried about "code being corrupted during our sessions." (1) **GHOST WRITE** — the status update at clockIn lines 1226-1233 (pre-v1.33) wrote `repair_orders.status='In Progress'` with ZERO audit_log entry whenever the prior status was anything else. Production audit (Q1 ghost-write enumerator, Session 71) returned 16 cross-RO mismatch rows — 11 of 16 (69%) trace to this single line: Ed Gordon (PRVS-5B3D-B18E), Jeannie Hickman (PRVS-050D-2FD3), David Hensley (PRVS-4983-9548), Rick Hinton (PRVS-720F-A5D5), Neal Silvers (PRVS-0697-D204), Mark Saint Pe (PRVS-4897-2ECA), Steve & Alana Smith (PRVS-ST05-E47B), Dez Rock/Kyle Taylor (PRVS-7BE2-236F), Don Mullins (PRVS-418A-23A7), Roland's training RO PRVS-7CFE-2397, even PRVS-6020-CE43 (PRVS - SHOP OPERATIONS). (2) **WRONG CASING** — pre-v1.33 wrote `'In Progress'` (capital P), but `index.html`'s canonical value used by every status dropdown, filter button, `STATUS_PROGRESS_MAP`, `statusColorMap`, `ALL_STATUSES`, Spanish translation key (`'En Progreso'`), and stats filter is `'In progress'` (lowercase p). So every tech clock-in left a row that (a) rendered with default-gray badge (no `'In Progress'` entry in colorMap), (b) was missed by the In-Progress filter button, (c) undercounted the dashboard's in-progress stats, and (d) fell back to literal "In Progress" English for Spanish users. Smoking-gun audit-log evidence from Jeannie Hickman's RO showed Brandon (2026-04-06), Lynn (2026-04-14), and Bobby (2026-05-18 + 2026-05-22) had been MANUALLY RE-TYPING her status via the dropdown for SIX WEEKS to fix the casing each time — audit_log captured all four of their fixes; tech clock-in overwrites in between were silent until v1.33. **v1.33 fix (pure attribution + correctness, no behavior change):** `const IN_PROGRESS = 'In progress'` (canonical lowercase), snapshot `priorStatus` BEFORE the UPDATE, insert `audit_log` row with `field_changed='status'`, `old_value=priorStatus`, `new_value='In progress'`, `user_name='<tech> (auto via clock-in)'`, insert `notes` row with `type='ro_status'` and `⏱ AUTO-STATUS: from "<prior>" → "In progress" (set automatically when <tech> clocked in)` body. Both audit + note inserts wrapped in try/catch (non-fatal — the status flip itself remains the primary action). Version bumped in 3 places: header comment block, on-screen `.version` pill, `DOMContentLoaded` console.log. **No DB schema change required.** No behavior change visible to the tech — the RO still moves into "In progress" the moment they clock in; the only new behavior is the change is attributable in `audit_log` and visible in the RO Status Notes timeline. **Historical backfill ran 2026-05-22 immediately after deploy:** `UPDATE repair_orders SET status='In progress' WHERE status='In Progress' AND deleted_at IS NULL` normalized 21 capital-P rows; batch audit_log row attributed to `v1.33 historical casing normalization (Session 71)` documents the cleanup; final verification `SELECT COUNT(*) WHERE status='In Progress'` returned 0. **git blame attribution evidence** (preserved here for future sessions): `git blame -L 1226,1234 main -- checkin.html` shows all 9 lines authored by `b733fc98` (Roland Shepard, 2026-03-19 — "Restore checkin.html v1.26"). `git log --pickaxe-regex -S "status: 'In Progress'" -- checkin.html` returns exactly ONE commit, `b5ed919` (2026-03-08 — "Add files via upload"). `git log --pickaxe -S "writeAuditLog" -- checkin.html` returns ZERO results — no commit has ever added an audit-log call to checkin.html until v1.33. The bug pre-dates every Claude session. **Investigation scope (Session 71):** grep of every `.update('repair_orders')` site across all 7 HTML files (16 sites in index.html alone) + audit of all 10 Supabase edge functions (zero writes to `repair_orders` from any) + check of all SQL migrations for triggers on `repair_orders` (zero triggers). - ✅ **v1.417 — Lynn admin-button flakiness ROOT-CAUSE FIX (Step 2 fallback bypass of loadUserRoles) (2026-05-21, Session 70, commit `c9b21a8`)**: Lynn (Admin in user_roles + Sr Manager in staff, on v1.416 deployed code) reported only 2 buttons visible (Closed ROs + Time Off) the morning after v1.416 deployed. DB check confirmed her `user_roles.Admin` row was perfect (1 row, no duplicates, assigned 2026-04-11). v1.416 had hardened `loadUserRoles()` internals against missing/duplicate `users` rows — but a SECOND silent-demote bug remained. Investigation traced the cause to a code path that bypassed `loadUserRoles()` entirely: session-restore Step 2 ("Fall back to Google token if Supabase session gone", line ~10637) set `sessionRestoredFromCache = true` and called `updateViewModeDropdown()` directly. The Google One Tap prompt skip-condition keyed on that same flag (`if (!sessionRestoredFromCache) google.accounts.id.prompt();`) — so when Step 2 fired (Supabase JWT expired overnight, Google token still warm), the One Tap prompt was SKIPPED, the signInWithIdToken callback never fired, `supabaseSession` stayed null, `userRoles` stayed `[]`, and every `isAdmin()` / `hasRole()` gate failed silently. The `sessionRestoredFromCache` flag was meant to mean "we're logged in" but actually only meant "we restored *something* from cache" — true even when only a stale Google token had been restored without a Supabase session. Pattern fit Lynn's "intermittent over multiple days" symptom: Supabase JWTs default to ~1 hour with refresh window; tabs left open overnight can have a dead Supabase session but a still-warm Google token (1+ hour grace), triggering Step 2 instead of Step 1. **5 surgical edits to index.html:** (1) `getUserInfo()` line ~10539 now awaits `loadUserRoles()` before `updateViewModeDropdown()` so post-login first paint reflects real roles. (2) Step 2 fallback line ~10653 now awaits `loadUserRoles()` before `updateViewModeDropdown()` so even the anon-key path renders any role data it can read (defense-in-depth). (3) Callback skip line ~10802 narrowed from `if (sessionRestoredFromCache || supabaseSession)` to just `if (supabaseSession)` — only skip Supabase re-auth when a real auth session exists. (4) Post-`signInWithIdToken` success line ~10823 now wraps `await loadUserRoles(); updateViewModeDropdown(); updateAuthStatus(true);` in a try/catch so role-gated UI re-renders the moment Supabase auth comes back online. (5) One Tap prompt skip line ~10832 flipped from `!sessionRestoredFromCache` → `!supabaseSession` — prompt One Tap whenever Supabase auth isn't live, regardless of UI cache state. **The `sessionRestoredFromCache` flag is preserved** for non-auth uses (controls some UI hydration timing) but is no longer used as a proxy for "RBAC is active." worklist-report.html and customer-checkin.html unchanged — they don't have the Step 2 Google-only fallback path (they check Supabase session and redirect to index.html if missing). **Trace of the fixed flow for Lynn's morning case:** Step 2 fires → `loadUserRoles()` runs but returns `[]` (anon RLS blocks the auth-required reads) → `updateViewModeDropdown()` hides buttons momentarily → One Tap prompt fires (NEW v1.417 — was skipped in v1.416) → `auto_select` picks Lynn's account → callback fires with `id_token` → new skip condition allows proceed → `signInWithIdToken` succeeds → `supabaseSession` populated → `loadUserRoles()` re-runs with valid session → `userRoles = ['Admin', 'Sr Manager']` → `updateViewModeDropdown()` re-renders → admin buttons appear. - ✅ **v1.416 — Hardened loadUserRoles() against silent-demote bug (Lynn lost Work List access — first half of fix) (2026-05-19, Session 69 follow-up, commit `89059d9`)**: Roland shipped this directly from his Mac terminal between Session 69 (Brandon Insurance WO Writer, v1.415) and Session 70 (Lynn root-cause fix, v1.417) to address Lynn's initial missing-buttons report. Root cause identified as a pre-existing latent bug in `loadUserRoles()`: when the `users` table lookup-by-email returned 0 rows OR errored (e.g. missing row, duplicate row, RLS-blocked), the function early-returned and skipped BOTH the `user_roles` query AND the `staff`-table merge — leaving `userRoles = []` and hiding every role-gated header button (My Work List sidebar, Work List Report, Add to My List per-card, Admin Settings, Analytics, Recently Deleted, ER admin, Customer Check-In, Solar) without surfacing an error. Session 69 itself didn't touch any of this code; the regression was exposed by some change to Lynn's `users`-row state. **Fix:** split `loadUserRoles()` into two INDEPENDENT role sources — (1) `user_roles` via `users.id` lookup, wrapped in its own try/catch so a missing/duplicate users row no longer aborts the whole function; (2) `staff`-table merge, runs UNCONDITIONALLY and maps `staff.role` → 'Sr Manager' / 'Manager' / 'Tech' even when `user_roles` failed. Switched the staff query from `.single()` to `.maybeSingle()` so 0 rows returns a quiet null instead of a 406. Both sources feed a single `mergedRoles` array that becomes `userRoles`. **Net effect:** real staffers with a valid `staff` row keep their role-derived buttons even when their `users` row is missing, duplicate, or RLS-blocked. Lynn gets 'Sr Manager' from staff regardless, restoring My Work List sidebar + Add to My List + Customer Check-In + Solar. **Admin restoration still requires a valid `user_roles.Admin` row** — GH#41 tracked the DB verification step. Same defensive pattern applied to worklist-report.html (v1.13 → v1.14) and customer-checkin.html (v1.6 → v1.7) — analytics.html, time-off.html, closed-ros.html use a safer `if (userRow?.id)` guard already and don't have this exact bug (flagged for cleanup pass anyway). **What v1.416 did NOT fix** — and what Session 70 / v1.417 had to address — was the SECOND silent-demote path: session-restore Step 2 (Google-only fallback) bypassed `loadUserRoles()` entirely. See v1.417 entry above for the rest of the story.

Work Orders + Photo Lightbox use fully inline styles — those were fine. **Fix:** (1) `.modal-overlay` backdrop bumped from `rgba(0,0,0,0.8)` → `rgba(0,0,0,0.88)` + added `backdrop-filter: blur(3px)` + `-webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(3px)`. (2) Added new `.modal-content` CSS rule: `background: var(--bg-surface)`, `border: 1px solid var(--border-color)`, `border-radius: 16px`, `padding: 28px`, `box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg)`, `animation: slideUp 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)` — matching the `.modal` class pattern. Inline `max-width`/`max-height` overrides on each modal instance continue to apply on top. Fix is centrally applied — all 5 affected modals get opaque backgrounds automatically. Roland confirmed: "Looks great. Both modals are updated and easier to read."
- ✅ **send-parts-report v1.7→v1.8 — Parts Report estimate bug fixed (2026-04-28, Session 59, commit `521aeb9`)**: Bobby reported the morning parts report was showing 5 ROs with `parts_status='estimate'` in the "Open Parts Requests" Section 1 — estimate-only parts requests are for quoting purposes and Bobby doesn't need to order them. Root cause: Section 1 query only excluded `parts_status='received'`; `'estimate'` status was not excluded. Fix: added two filters to Section 1 query: `.not("parts_status", "eq", "estimate")` and `.is("deleted_at", null)` (also excludes soft-deleted ROs). Version bumped v1.7→v1.8 in summary response. - ✅ **Work Orders RLS — Sr Manager bypass via `is_sr_manager_or_admin()` (2026-04-28, Session 59, commit `042d723`)**: Kevin McHenry (Sr Manager) reported no access to Work Orders — couldn't see "My List", "Add to My List", or build/edit project lists. DB diagnostic confirmed Kevin's RBAC was perfect (correct role in user_roles + roles tables). RLS policy inspection (`pg_policies`) revealed the root cause: all 5 write policies on `service_work_orders` (swo_insert, swo_update, swo_delete) and `service_tasks` (st_insert, st_update, st_delete) only checked `is_silo_manager()` — which returns false for any user with a NULL `service_silo` in the `staff` table. Sr Managers (Roland, Ryan, Kevin) all have NULL silo. No admin/sr_manager bypass existed on any policy. Fix: new `is_sr_manager_or_admin()` SECURITY DEFINER function (checks `user_roles → roles` for names 'Sr Manager' or 'Admin', not the `staff` table) + all 5 policies updated to include `OR is_sr_manager_or_admin()`. Migration `fix_wo_rls_sr_manager_bypass.sql` committed via GitHub MCP. Roland ran SQL ("Success. No rows returned"). Kevin instructed to hard refresh + sign out/in.

Insert via authenticated session. **ER#1 wiring:** `customer-checkin.html` persists `planned_dropoff_date` (from `leadDropoffDate` in lead mode OR `scheduledDropoffDate` in dropoff/scheduled mode) AND auto-INSERTs a reminder row scheduled for `planned_dropoff_date - 1 day at 13:00 UTC` (8 AM CDT) — recipients hardcoded to `repair@patriotsrvservices.com` for v1 (anon-key path can't lookup staff). Edit RO modal: new "Planned Drop Off Date" field; on save, change cascade cancels existing pending auto-reminders (`UPDATE status='cancelled'`) and inserts a fresh one with the new scheduled_at + silo-manager recipients (looked up via `_staffCache`). - ✅ **GH#29 Status-change bug fix — 13-site UUID-first lookup (2026-04-18, Session 51, v1.408)**: Managers and techs reported status changes not sticking. Root cause: 13 write-path lookups resolved `currentFilteredData[idx] → currentData` via `findIndex(item => item.customerName === ro.customerName && item.dateReceived === ro.dateReceived)` — with `(name, date)` dupes, `findIndex` returned the FIRST match, every write silently targeted the wrong row. Affected: updateROStatus/Urgency/Progress, editField, uploadPhoto/Document, setMainPhoto, archiveRO, openScheduleModal/confirmSchedule/proceedWithSchedule, openPartsModal, openEditRO. Fix: `ro._supabaseId ? currentData.findIndex(item => item._supabaseId === ro._supabaseId) : fallback(name+date)`. Applied via `patch_status_bug.py` Python regex (8 `item =>` sites + 5 `d =>` sites). Roland confirmed fix on dupe scenario AND unique ROs. Commit: `0a486e4`.
- ✅ **GH#29c Status-bug root-cause investigation (2026-04-18, Session 51)**: After v1.408 shipped, confirmed Supabase RLS policies permissive (`authenticated_full_access: ALL qual=true` + anon SELECT only) — silent-RLS theory dead. Roland's post-fix test showed unique-RO status changes stick. Leading hypothesis: v1.408 dupe-lookup fix resolved all staff-reported stickiness. Monitoring TODO (`GH#29c`) with DevTools Network playbook logged for if it resurfaces. Belt-and-suspenders follow-up: extend `.select()` + row-count assertion (already on GH#30 soft-delete) to all 13 v1.408 write sites. Not yet done.

- ✅ **Duplicate ro_id 409 fix (v1.278)** — `generateROId()` is a deterministic 32-bit hash; same customer+RV+date (or any hash collision) produced identical IDs causing a Supabase 409 Conflict on insert. Added `async generateUniqueROId(name, rv, date)` which calls `generateROId()` then checks Supabase with `.maybeSingle()` before committing — if collision detected, appends `-2` through `-9`, then falls back to a base-36 timestamp suffix. Updated `appendToSupabase` to `await generateUniqueROId()`. Added try/catch at the New RO form submit handler so errors produce a user-visible alert instead of a silent uncaught promise rejection.
- ✅ **Video upload support (v1.279)** — Added `isVideoUrl(url)` helper (checks .mp4/.mov/.avi/.mkv/.webm/.m4v/.3gp extensions). `uploadPhoto` now accepts `image/*,video/*` and the image-only `continue` filter was widened to allow `video/` MIME types. Thumbnail grid renders a dark `🎬 VIDEO` tile for video URLs instead of a broken `<img>`. Lightbox renders `<video controls autoplay>` for videos and suppresses "Set as Main" (videos can't be an RO's main photo). Email modal shows videos as disabled/non-checkable with a `🎬 Video (not emailable)` label. "Add New Photo" button renamed "Add Photo / Video".
- ✅ **Fix RO insert race condition (v1.280)** — Replaced check-then-insert pattern (`generateUniqueROId` with pre-SELECT) with optimistic insert loop (`generateROIdCandidates` returns base + -2..-9 + timestamp fallback). `appendToSupabase` now tries each candidate in sequence; on `error.code === '23505'` it advances to the next; any other error is re-thrown. Eliminates the TOCTOU race where concurrent submits could both pass the pre-check and both fail on insert. Also added submit button disable/re-enable around the save call to prevent double-submissions.
- ✅ **Fix roId scope bug (v1.281)** — `appendToSupabase` optimistic insert loop used `for (const roId of candidates)`; the `console.log` after the loop referenced `roId` which is block-scoped to the loop body, causing `ReferenceError: roId is not defined`. Fixed by changing `console.log('✅ New RO saved:', roId)` to `console.log('✅ New RO saved:', data.ro_id)`.
- ✅ **Duplicate RO Manager (v1.282)** — `getBaseROId(roId)` strips `-2`/`-3`/`-XXXX` suffixes via regex to find the base PRVS hash. `findDuplicateGroups()` groups `currentData` by base ID and returns groups with 2+ members. Admin-only `🔗 Merge Dupes` button in header (hidden until dupes detected) with red badge count. `openDuplicateManager()` modal shows each group with radio buttons to pick the master RO. `executeDupeMerge()` reassigns foreign keys on `notes`, `parts`, `time_logs`, `insurance_scans`, `audit_log` tables; merges `photo_library` arrays; copies `rvPhotoUrl` from duplicate to master if master has none; DELETEs duplicate `repair_orders` rows; reloads data.
- ✅ **Fix isAdmin() timing bug for Merge Dupes button (v1.282b)** — `getUserInfo()` called with no Google token sets `currentUser = { email: 'unknown@user.com' }`. The `if (!currentUser)` guard in session restore then skips overwriting it with the real email. `isAdmin()` checks `currentUser.email` which is wrong. Fix: post-load dupe check now also checks `supabaseSession?.user?.email` directly against `ADMIN_EMAILS` (`const _sessionEmail = (supabaseSession?.user?.email || '').toLowerCase(); const _isAdminNow = isAdmin() || ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(_sessionEmail)`). Added `console.log('🔗 Dupe check: X duplicate(s) found, button shown/hidden')` for debugging.
- ✅ **Fix "Date RV Arrived on Lot" not saving (v1.283)** — `updateROInSupabase()` had `date_arrived` missing from its Supabase `.update()` payload. Value was correctly read from the Edit RO form into `formData.dateArrived` but silently dropped before the DB write. Fix: added `date_arrived: formData.dateArrived || null` to the payload. Explains why it appeared to work on some ROs (those whose date was auto-set via the status-change path) but failed on others (manually entered via Edit RO).
- ✅ **Parts chip states — three-state system (v1.284, GH#14)** — `parts_status` column added to `repair_orders` (CHECK constraint: 'sourcing', 'outstanding', 'received'). Auto-flip: `markPartReceived()` checks if all parts received/installed and calls `setPartsStatus(..., 'received')` automatically. Filter buttons: `ps-sourcing`, `ps-outstanding`, `ps-received`. `submitPartsRequest` sets `parts_status='outstanding'`. Backward compat with legacy `has_open_parts_request` boolean.

| v1.429 (branch) | 2026-05-29 | **Modularization Phase 4.5-E — defer CDN tags + delete final 3 CDN-coupled inline auth fns + v1.417 Step-2 backfill (Session 82, branch `refactor/auth-phase-4.5-e` — NOT YET MERGED to pre-prod or main).** Three surgical commits. **Commit 1 — Phase 4.5-E architecture:** index.html L15851 gsi/client tag `async defer` → `defer` (dropping `async` because async overrides defer's in-document-order execution); L15854 api.js tag bare → `defer`.
